    <body>
      <div n="1" type="sthāna">
        <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 32-end]</head>
       <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

					<l xml:id="SS.1.32.1">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.32.1</label>
						<caesura/>athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.32.2">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.32.2</label>
						<caesura/>yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.32.3-4</label>
						<caesura/> svabhāvasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām anyabhāvitvaṃ maraṇāya | tad
						yathā- śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ, kṛṣṇānāṃ śuklatā, raktānām anyavarṇatvaṃ,
						sthirāṇāṃ mṛdutvaṃ , mṛdūnāṃ sthiratā, calānāmacalatvaṃ, acalānāṃ calatā,
						pṛthūnāṃ saṅkṣiptatvaṃ, saṅkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutā, dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ,
						hrasvānāṃ dīrghatā, apatanadharmiṇāṃ patanadharmitvaṃ ,
						patanadharmiṇāmapatanadharmitvamakasmāt, śaity
						auṣṇyasnaigdhyaraukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇyāvasādanaṃ cāṅgānām ||3|| svebhyaḥ
						sthānebhyaḥ
						śarīraikadeśānāmavastrastotkṣiptabhrāntāvakṣiptapatitavimuktanirgatāntargatagurulaghutvāni,
						pravālavarṇavyaṅgaprādurbhāvo vā'pyakasmāt, sirāṇāṃ ca darśanaṃ lalāṭe,
						nāsāvaṃśe vā piḍakotpattiḥ , lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle svedaḥ, netrarogādvinā
						vā'śrupravṛttiḥ, gomayacūrṇaprakāśasya vā rajaso darśanamuttamāṅge nilayanaṃ
						vā kapotakaṅkakākaprabhṛtīnāṃ, mūtrapurīṣavṛddhirabhuñjānānāṃ, tatpraṇāśo vā
						bhuñjānānāṃ, stanamūlahṛdayor aḥsu ca śūlotpattayaḥ, madhye śūnatvamanteṣu
						parimlāyitvaṃ viparyayo vā, tathā'rdhāṅge śvayathuḥ śoṣo 'ṅgapakṣayor vā,
						naṣṭahīnavikalavikṛtasvaratā vā, vivarṇapuṣpaprādurbhāvo vā
						dantamukhanakhaśarīreṣu, yasya vā'psu kaphapurīṣaretāṃsi nimajjanti, yasya
						vā dṛṣṭimaṇḍale bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇyālokyante, snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo
						bhāti, yaś ca durbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyāṃ pīḍyate, kāsamānaśca
						tṛṣṇābhibhūtaḥ, kṣīṇaśchardibhaktadveṣayuktaḥ saphenapūyarudhirodvāmī
						hatasvaraḥ śūlābhipannaś ca manuṣyaḥ, śūnakaracaraṇavadanaḥkṣīṇo 'nnadveṣī
						srastapiṇḍikāṃsapāṇipādo jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ, yas tu pūrvāhṇe bhuktamaparāhṇe
						chardayatyavidagdhamatisāryate vā sa śvāsānmriyate, bastavadvilapan yaśca
						bhūmau patati srastamuṣkaḥ, stabdhameḍhro bhagnagrīvaḥ pranaṣṭamehanaśca
						manuṣyaḥ, prāgviśuṣyamāṇāhṛdaya ārdraśarīraḥ, yaś ca loṣṭaṃ loṣṭenābhihanti
						kāṣṭhaṃ kāṣṭhena, tṛṇāni vā chinatti, adharoṣṭhaṃ daśati, uttaroṣṭhaṃ vā
						leḍhi, āluñcati vā karṇau keśāṃśca; devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyāṃś ca dveṣṭi,
						yasya vakrānuvakragā grahā garhitasthānagatāḥ pīḍayanti, janmarkṣaṃ vā,
						yasyolkāśanibhyāmabhihanyate horā vā,
						gṛhadāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbhāvo
						veti ||4|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.32.5">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.32.5</label>
						<caesura/> bhavanti cātra <caesura/>cikitsyamānaḥ samyak ca vikāro yo
						'bhivardhate | <caesura/> prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya lakṣaṇaṃ tadgatāyuṣaḥ ||5|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.32.6">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.32.6</label>
						<caesura/> nivartate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ | <caesura/>na
						cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati ||6||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.32.7">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.32.7</label>
						<caesura/> etāny ariṣṭarūpāṇi samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak |
						<caesura/>sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣāyāṃ sa rājñaḥ sammato bhavet ||7|| </l>

					<p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne svabhāvavipratipattirnāma
						dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||32||</p>
				</div>


				<div n="33" type="adhyāya">

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.1">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.1</label>
						<caesura/>athāto 'vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.2">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.2</label>
						<caesura/>yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.3">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.3</label>
						<caesura/> upadravais tu ye juṣṭā vyādhayo yānty avāryatām |
						<caesura/>rasāyanād vinā vatsa! tān śṛṇv ekamanā mama ||3|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.4">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.4</label>
						<caesura/> vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭham arśo bhagandaram |
						<caesura/>aśmarī mūḍhagarbhaś ca tathaivodaram aṣṭamam ||4|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.5">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.5</label>
						<caesura/> aṣṭāv ete prakṛtyaiva duścikitsyā mahāgadāḥ
						<caesura/>prāṇamāṃsakṣayaḥ śoṣastṛṣṇā cchardirjvaras tathā ||5||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.6">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.6</label>
						<caesura/> atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca hikkā śvāsas tathaiva ca | <caesura/>etair
						upadravair juṣṭān sarvāneva vivarjayet ||6|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.7">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.7</label>
						<caesura/> śūnaṃ suptatvacaṃ bhagnaṃ kampādhmānanipīḍitam | <caesura/>naraṃ
						rujārtamantaś ca vātavyādhir vināśayet ||7|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.8">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.8</label>
						<caesura/> yathoktopadravāviṣṭam atiprasrutam eva vā |
						<caesura/>piḍakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavam ||8|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.9">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.9</label>
						<caesura/> prabhinna prasrutāṅgaṃ ca raktanetraṃ hatasvaram |
						<caesura/>pañcakarmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hantīha kuṣṭhinam ||9|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.10">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.10</label>
						<caesura/> tṛṣṇārocakaśūlārtam atiprasrutaśoṇitam | <caesura/>
						śophātīsārasaṃyuktam arśovyādhir vināśayet ||10|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.11">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.11</label>
						<caesura/> vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca | <caesura/>bhagandarāt
						prasravanti yasya taṃ parivarjayet ||11|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.12">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.12</label>
						<caesura/> praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ ruddhamūtraṃ ruganvitam | <caesura/>aśmarī
						kṣapayatyāśu sikatā śarkarānvitā ||12|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.13">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.13</label>
						<caesura/> garbhakoṣaparāsaṅgo makkallo yonisaṃvṛtiḥ | <caesura/>hanyāt
						striyaṃ mūḍhagarbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ ||13|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.14">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.14</label>
						<caesura/> pārśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaśophātīsārapīḍitam | <caesura/>viriktaṃ
						pūryamāṇaṃ ca varjayed udarārditam ||14|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.15">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.15</label>
						<caesura/> yas tāmyati visañjñaś ca śete nipatito 'pi vā |
						<caesura/>śītārdito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ ||15|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.16">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.16</label>
						<caesura/> yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṅghātaśūlavān | <caesura/>nityaṃ
						vaktreṇa cocchvasyāttaṃ jvaro hanti mānavam ||16||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.17">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.17</label>
						<caesura/> hikkāśvāsapipāsārtaṃ mūḍhaṃ vibhrāntalocanam |
						<caesura/>santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayati jvaraḥ ||17|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.18">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.18</label>
						<caesura/> āvilākṣaṃ pratāmyantaṃ nidrāyuktamatīva ca |
						<caesura/>kṣīṇaśoṇitamāṃsaṃ ca naraṃ nāśayati jvaraḥ ||18|</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.19">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.19</label>
						<caesura/> śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ kṣīṇaṃ jvaranipīḍitam | <caesura/>viśeṣeṇa
						naraṃ vṛddhamatīsāro vināśayet ||19|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.20">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.20</label>
						<caesura/> śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāramūrdhvaśvāsanipīḍitam | <caesura/>kṛcchreṇa
						bahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavam ||20|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.21">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.21</label>
						<caesura/> śvāsaśūlapipāsānnavidveṣagranthimūḍhatāḥ | <caesura/>bhavanti
						durbalatvaṃ ca gulmino mṛtyumeṣyataḥ ||21|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.22">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.22</label>
						<caesura/> ādhmātaṃ baddhaniṣyandaṃ chardihikkātṛḍanvitam |
						<caesura/>rujāśvāsasamāviṣṭaṃ vidradhirnāśayennaram ||22|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.23">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.23</label>
						<caesura/> pāṇḍudantanakho yaś ca pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ |
						<caesura/>pāṇḍusaṅghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vinaśyati ||23|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.24">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.24</label>
						<caesura/> lohitaṃ chardayed yas tu bahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ | <caesura/>raktānāṃ
						ca diśāṃ draṣṭā raktapittī vinaśyati ||24|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.25">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.25</label>
						<caesura/> avāṅmukhastūnmukho vā kṣīṇamāṃsabalo naraḥ | <caesura/>jāgariṣṇur
						asandeham unmādena vinaśyati ||25|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.33.26">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.33.26</label>
						<caesura/> bahuśo 'pasmarantaṃ tu prakṣīṇaṃ calitabhruvam |
						<caesura/>netrābhyāṃ ca vikurvāṇam apasmāro vināśayet ||26|| </l>

					<p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne 'vāraṇīyo nāma
						trayastriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||33|| </p>
				</div>
				<div n="34" type="adhyāya">

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.1">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.1</label> athāto yuktasenīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.2">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.3">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.3</label>
						<caesura/> nṛpater yuktasenasya parānabhijigīṣataḥ | <caesura/>bhiṣajā
						rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yathā tadupadekṣyate ||3|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.4">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.4</label>
						<caesura/> vijigīṣuḥ sahāmātyairyātrāyuktaḥ prayatnataḥ |
						<caesura/>rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇa viṣād eva narādhipaḥ ||4|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.5">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.5</label>
						<caesura/> panthānam udakaṃ chāyāṃ bhaktaṃ yavasam indhanam |
						dūṣayantyarayastac ca jānīyācchodhayettathā ||5|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.6">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.6</label>
						<caesura/> tasya liṅgaṃ cikitsā ca kalpasthāne pravakṣyate <caesura/>
						ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam atharvāṇaḥ pracakṣate ||6|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.7">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.7</label>
						<caesura/> tatraikaḥ kālasaṃyuktaḥ śeṣā āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ <caesura/>
						doṣāgantujamṛtyubhyo rasamantraviśāradau ||7|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.8">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.8</label>
						<caesura/> rakṣetāṃ nṛpatiṃ nityaṃ yattau vaidyapurohitau <caesura/> brahmā
						vedāṅgam aṣṭāṅgam āyurvedam abhāṣata ||8|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.9">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.9</label>
						<caesura/> purohitamate tasmād varteta bhiṣag ātmavān <caesura/> saṅkaraḥ
						sarvavarṇānāṃ praṇāśo dharmakarmaṇām ||9|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.10">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.10</label>
						<caesura/> prajānām api cocchittirnṛpavyasanahetutaḥ <caesura/> puruṣāṇāṃ
						nṛpāṇāṃ ca kevalaṃ tulyamūrtitā ||10|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.11">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.11</label>
						<caesura/> ājñā tyāgaḥ kṣamā dhairyaṃ vikramaś cāpy amānuṣaḥ | <caesura/>
						tasmād devam ivābhīkṣṇaṃ vāṅmanaḥkarmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ ||11|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.12">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.12</label>
						<caesura/> cintayen nṛpatiṃ vaidyaḥ śreyāṃsīcchan vicakṣaṇaḥ <caesura/>
						skandhāvāre ca mahati rājagehādanantaram ||12|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.13">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.13</label>
						<caesura/> bhavetsannihito vaidyaḥ sarvopakaraṇānvitaḥ | 
						<caesura/>tatrasthamenaṃ dhvajavadyaśaḥkhyātisamucchritam ||13|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.14">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.14</label>
						<caesura/> upasarpantyamohena viṣaśalyāmayārditāḥ | 
						<caesura/>svatantrakuśalo 'nyeṣu śāstrārtheṣv abahiṣkṛtaḥ ||14||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.34.15">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.34.15</label>
						<caesura/> vaidyo dhvaja ivābhāti nṛpatadvidyapūjitaḥ <caesura/> vaidyo

						<caesura/> atha punarāyuṣo vijñānārtham
						aṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇasārānupadekṣyāmaḥ | tatrāṅgāny
						antarādhisakthibāhuśirāṃsi, tad avayavāḥ pratyaṅgānīti | tatra, svair
						aṅgulaiḥ pādāṅguṣṭhapradeśinyau dvyaṅgulāyate ; pradeśinyāstu
						madhyamānāmikākaniṣṭhikā yathottaraṃ pañcamabhāgahīnāḥ; caturaṅgulāyate
						pañcāṅgulavistṛte</l>


					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.12cd">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.12cd</label> prapadapādatale;
						pañcacaturaṅgulāyatavistṛtā pārṣṇiḥ; caturdaśāṅgulāyataḥ pādaḥ;
						caturdaśāṅgulapariṇāhāni pādagulphajaṅghājānumadhyāni; aṣṭādaśāṅgulā jaṅghā,
						jānūpariṣṭācca dvātriṃśadaṅgulam, ete pañcāśat; jaṅghāyāmasamāvūrū;
						dvyaṅgulāni vṛṣaṇacibukadaśananāsāpuṭabhāgakarṇamūlabhrūnayanāntarāṇi;
						caturaṅgulāni mehanavadanāntaranāsākarṇalalāṭagrīvocchrāyadṛṣṭyantarāṇi;
						dvādaśāṅgulāni
						bhagavistāramehananābhihṛdayagrīvāstanāntaramukhāyāmamaṇibandhaprakoṣṭhasthaulyāni;
						indrabastipariṇāhāṃsapīṭhakūrparāntarāyāmaḥ ṣoḍaśāṅgulaḥ; caturviṃśatyaṅgulo
						hastaḥ; dvātriṃśadaṅgulaparimāṇau bhujau; dvātriṃśatpariṇāhāvūrū;
						maṇibandhakūrparāntaraṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulaṃ; talaṃ ṣaṭcaturaṅgulāyāmavistāram;
						aṅguṣṭhamūlapradeśinīśravaṇāpāṅgāntaramadhyamāṅgulyau pañcāṅgule;
						ardhapañcāṅgule pradeśinyanāmike; sārdhatryaṅgulau kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhau;
						caturviṃśativistārapariṇāhaṃ mukhagrīvaṃ; tribhāgāṅgulavistārā
						nāsāpuṭamaryādā; nayanatribhāgapariṇāhā tārakā; navamastārakāṃśo dṛṣṭiḥ;
						keśāntamastakāntaramekādaśāṅgulaṃ; mastakādavaṭukeśānto daśāṅgulaḥ;
						karṇāvaṭvantaraṃ caturdaśāṅgulaṃ; puruṣoraḥpramāṇavistīrṇā strīśroṇiḥ;
						aṣṭādaśāṅgulavistāramuraḥ; tatpramāṇā puruṣasya kaṭī; saviṃśamaṅgulaśataṃ
						puruṣāyāma iti ||12|| </l>

						<caesura/> vyādhiviśeṣās tu prāgabhihitāḥ; sarva evaite trividhāḥ- sādhyā,
						yāpyāḥ, pratyākhyeyāś ca | tatraitān bhūyastridhā parīkṣeta-
						kimayamaupasargikaḥ, prākkevalaḥ, anyalakṣaṇa iti | tatra, aupasargiko nāma
						yaḥ pūrvotpannaṃ vyādhiṃ jaghanyakālajāto vyādhirupasṛjati, sa tanmūla
						evopadravasañjñaḥ; prākkevalo nāma yaḥ prāgevotpanno vyādhirapūrvarūpo
						'nupadravaśca; anyalakṣaṇo nāma yo bhaviṣyadvyādhikhyāpakaḥ, sa
						pūrvarūpasañjñaḥ | tatra, sopadravamanyonyāvirodhenopakrameta, balavantam
						upadravaṃ vā; prākkevalaṃ yathāsvaṃ pratikurvīta; anyalakṣaṇe tvād ivyādhau

						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.24</label>
						<caesura/> prāgabhihito 'gnir annasya pācakaḥ | sa caturvidho bhavati-
						doṣānabhipanna ekaḥ, vikriyām āpannas trividho bhavati- viṣamo vātena, tīkṣṇaḥ
						pittena, mandaḥ śleṣmaṇā, caturthaḥ samaḥ sarvasāmyāditi | tatra, yo
						yathākālam upayuktamannaṃ samyak pacati sa samaḥ, samairdoṣaiḥ; yaḥ kadācit
						samyak pacati,
						kadācidādhmānaśūlodāvartātisārajaṭharagauravāntrakūjanapravāhaṇāni kṛtvā, sa
						viṣamaḥ; yaḥ prabhūtam apy upayuktam annam āśu pacati sa tīkṣṇaḥ, sa
						evābhivardhamāno 'tyagnirity ābhāṣyate, sa muhur muhuḥ
						prabhūtam apy upayuktam annam āśutaraṃ pacati, pākānte ca
						galatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpā ñjanayati;
						yastvalpamapyupayuktamudaraśirogauravakāsaśvāsaprasekacchardigātrasadanāni
						kṛtvā mahatā kālena pacati, sa mandaḥ ||24|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.29">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.29</label>
						<caesura/> vayas tu trividhaṃ- bālyaṃ, madhyaṃ, vṛddham iti |
						tatronaṣoḍaśavarṣīyā bālāḥ | te trividhāḥ- kṣīrapāḥ, kṣīrānnādā, annādā iti
						| teṣu saṃvatsaraparāḥ kṣīrapāḥ, dvisaṃvatsaraparāḥ kṣīrānnādāḥ, parato
						'nnādā iti | ṣoḍaśasaptatyor antare madhyaṃ vayaḥ | tasya vikalpo- vṛddhiḥ,
						yauvanaṃ, sampūrṇatā, parihāṇiriti | tatra, āviṃśatervṛddhiḥ, ātriṃśato
						yauvanam, ācatvāriṃśataḥ sarvadhātvindriyabalavīryasampūrṇatā, ata
						ūrdhvamīṣatparihāṇiryāvat saptatiriti | saptaterūrdhvaṃ
						kṣīyamāṇadhātvindriyabalavīryotsāhamahanyahani valīpalitakhālity ajuṣṭaṃ
						kāsaśvāsaprabhṛtibhir upadravairabhibhūyamānaṃ sarvakriyāsvasamarthaṃ
						jīrṇāgāramivābhivṛṣṭamavasīdantaṃ vṛddhamācakṣate ||29|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.35">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.35</label>
						<caesura/> balam abhihitaguṇaṃ; daurbalyaṃ tu svabhāvadoṣajarādibhir
						avekṣitavyam | 
						<caesura/>yasmād balavataḥ sarvakriyāpravṛttis tasmād balam eva
						pradhānam adhikaraṇānām ||35|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.36">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.36</label>
						<caesura/> kecit kṛśāḥ prāṇavantaḥ sthūlāś cālpabalā narāḥ | 
						<caesura/>tasmāt sthiratvaṃ vyāyāmairbalaṃ vaidyaḥ pratarkayet ||36|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.37">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.37</label>
						<caesura/> sattvaṃ tu vyasanābhyudayakriyādisthāneṣv aviklavakaram ||37|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.38">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.38</label>
						<caesura/> sattvavān sahate sarvaṃ saṃstabhyātmānamātmanā | 
						<caesura/>rājasaḥ stabhyamāno 'nyaiḥ sahate naiva tāmasaḥ ||38|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.39">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.39</label>
						<caesura/> sātmyāni tu
						deśakālajātyṛturogavyāyāmodakadivāsvapnarasaprabhṛtīni prakṛtiviruddhāny api
						yāny abādhakarāṇi bhavanti ||39|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.40">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.40</label>
						<caesura/> yo rasaḥ kalpate yasya sukhāyaiva niṣevitaḥ | 
						<caesura/>vyāyāmajātamanyadvā tat sātmyam iti nirdiśet ||40|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.41">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.41</label>
						<caesura/> prakṛtiṃ bheṣajaṃ copariṣṭād vakṣyāmaḥ ||41|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.42">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.42</label>
						<caesura/> deśastvānūpo jāṅgalaḥ sādhāraṇa iti | tatra,
						bahūdakanimnonnatanadīvarṣagahano mṛduśītānilo bahumahāparvatavṛkṣo
						mṛdusukumāropacitaśarīramanuṣyaprāyaḥ kaphavātarogabhūyiṣṭhaś cānūpaḥ;
						ākāśasamaḥ praviralālpakaṇṭakivṛkṣaprāyo 'lpavarṣaprasravaṇodapānodakaprāya
						uṣṇadāruṇavātaḥ praviralālpaśailaḥ sthirakṛśaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo
						vātapittarogabhūyiṣṭhaś ca jāṅgalaḥ; ubhayadeśalakṣaṇaḥ sādhāraṇa iti ||42|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.43">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.43</label>
						<caesura/> bhavanti cātra
						<caesura/>samāḥ sādhāraṇe yasmācchītavarṣoṣmamārutāḥ |
						<caesura/>doṣāṇāṃ samatā jantostasmāt sādhāraṇo mataḥ ||43|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.44">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.44</label>
						<caesura/> na tathā balavantaḥ syurjalajā vā sthalāhṛtāḥ | 
						<caesura/>svadeśe nicitā doṣā anyasmin kopam āgatāḥ ||44|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.45">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.45</label>
						<caesura/> ucite vartamānasya nāsti deśakṛtaṃ bhayam | ૉ
						<caesura/>āhārasvapnaceṣṭādau taddeśasya guṇe sati ||45||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.46">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.46</label>
						<caesura/> deśaprakṛtisātmyartu viparīto 'cirotthitaḥ | 
						<caesura/>sampattau bhiṣagādīnāṃ balasattvāyuṣāṃ tathā ||46||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.47">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.47</label>
						<caesura/> kevalaḥ samadehāgneḥ sukhasādhyatamo gadaḥ | 
						<caesura/>ato 'nyathā tvasādhyaḥ syāt kṛcchro vyāmiśralakṣaṇaḥ ||47||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.48">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.48</label>
						<caesura/> kriyāyās tu guṇālābhe kriyām anyāṃ prayojayet | 
						<caesura/>pūrvasyāṃ śāntavegāyāṃ na kriyāsaṅkaro hitaḥ ||48|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.49">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.49</label>
						<caesura/> guṇālābhe 'pi sapadi yadi saiva kriyā hitā | 
						<caesura/>kartavyaiva tadā vyādhiḥ kṛcchrasādhyatamo yadi ||49|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.35.50">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.35.50</label>
						<caesura/> ya evam enaṃ vidhim ekarūpaṃ bibharti kālādivaśena dhīmān | 
						<caesura/>sa mṛtyupāśāñ jagato gadaughāñ chinatti bhaiṣajyaparaśvadhena ||50|| </l>

					<p ana="trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne āturopakramaṇīyo nāma
						pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||35|| </p>
				</div>
				<div n="36" type="adhyāya">
					<!--<note>There are large differences
                            		between the Ācārya 1931 and 1938 editions version of
                            		Cakrapāṇidatta's commentary on this adhyāya.</note>-->
					
					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.1"> athāto bhūmipravibhāgīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
					
					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.2"> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>
					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.3">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.3</label>
						<caesura/>
						śvabhraśarkarāśmaviṣamavalmīkaśmaśānāghātanadevatāyatanasikatābhir
						anupahatāmanūṣarāmabhaṅgurāmadūrodakāṃ snigdhāṃ prarohavatīṃ mṛdvīṃ sthirāṃ
						samāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ gaurīṃ lohitāṃ vā bhūmim auṣadhagrahaṇāya parīkṣeta | tasyāṃ
						jātamapi kṛmiviṣaśastrātapapavanadahanatoyasambādhamārgairanupahatamekarasaṃ
						puṣṭaṃ pṛthvavagāḍhamūlamudīcyāṃ cauṣadhamādadītetyeṣa bhūmiparīkṣāviśeṣaḥ
						sāmānyaḥ ||3|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.4">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.4</label>
						<caesura/> viśeṣatas tu tatra, aśmavatī sthirā gurvī śyāmā kṛṣṇā vā
						sthūlavṛkṣaśasyaprāyā svaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; snigdhā śītalā''sannodakā
						snigdhaśasyatṛṇakomalavṛkṣaprāyā śuklā'mbuguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; nānāvarṇā
						laghvaśmavatī praviralālpapāṇḍuvṛkṣaprarohā'gniguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; rūkṣā
						bhasmarāsabhavarṇā tanuvṛkṣālparasakoṭaravṛkṣaprāyā'nilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā; mṛdvī
						samā śvabhravatyavyaktarasajalā sarvato 'sāravṛkṣā mahāparvatavṛkṣaprāyā
						śyāmā cākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā ||4|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.5">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.5</label>
						<caesura/> atra kecid āhur ācāryāḥ- prāvṛḍvarṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmeṣu
						yathāsaṅkhyaṃ mūlapatratvakkṣīrasāraphalānyādadīteti; tat tu na samyak,
						saumyāgneyatvājjagataḥ | saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣvṛtuṣvādadīta,
						āgneyānyāgneyeṣu; evamavyāpannaguṇāni bhavanti | saumyāny auṣadhmani
						saumyeṣvṛtuṣu gṛhītāni somaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau
						jātānyatimadhurasnigdhaśītāni jāyante | etena śeṣaṃ vyākhyātam ||5|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.6">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.6</label>
						<caesura/> tatra pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau jātāni
						virecanadravyāṇyādadīta , agnyākāśamārutaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ vamanadravyāṇi,
						ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāmubhayatobhāgāni, ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃśamanāni,
						evaṃ balavattarāṇi bhavanti ||6|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.7">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.7</label>
						<caesura/> sarvāṇyeva cābhinavāni, anyatra madhughṛtaguḍapippalīviḍaṅgebhyaḥ
						||7||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.8">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.8</label>
						<caesura/> viḍaṅgaṃ pippalī kṣaudraṃ sarpiś cāpy anavaṃ hitam |
						śeṣam anyatv abhinavaṃ gṛhṇīyāddoṣavarjitam ||8|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.9">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.9</label>
						<caesura/> (sarvāṇyeva sakṣīrāṇi vīryavanti;) teṣāṃ
						asampattāvatikrāntasaṃvatsarāṇyādadīteti ||9|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.10">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.10</label>
						<caesura/> bhavanti cātra- gopālāstāpasā vyādhā ye cānye vanacāriṇaḥ |
						mūlāhārāś ca ye tebhyo bheṣajavyaktiriṣyate ||10|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.11">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.11</label>
						<caesura/> sarvāvayavasādhyeṣu palāśalavaṇādiṣu | vyavasthito na kālo 'sti
						tatra sarvo vidhīyate ||11|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.12">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.12</label>
						<caesura/> gandhavarṇarasopetā ṣaḍvidhā bhūmiriṣyate | tasmād
						bhūmisvabhāvena bījinaḥ ṣaḍrasāyutāḥ ||12|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.13">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.13</label>
						<caesura/> avyaktaḥ kila toyasya raso niścayaniścitaḥ | rasaḥ sa eva
						cāvyakto vyakto bhūmirasādbhavet ||13|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.14">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.14</label>
						<caesura/> sarvalakṣaṇasampannā bhūmiḥ sādhāraṇā smṛtā | dravyāṇi yatra
						tatraiva tadguṇāni viśeṣataḥ ||14|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.15">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.15</label>
						<caesura/> vigandhenāparāmṛṣṭamavipannaṃ rasādibhiḥ | navaṃ dravyaṃ purāṇaṃ
						vā grāhyamevaṃ vinirdiśet ||15|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.16">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.16</label>
						<caesura/> jaṅgamānāṃ vayaḥsthānāṃ raktaromanakhādikam | kṣīramūtrapurīṣāṇi
						jīrṇāhāreṣu saṃharet ||16|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.17">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.17</label>
						<caesura/> plotamṛdbhāṇḍaphalakaśaṅkuvinyastabheṣajam | praśastāyāṃ diśi
						śucau bheṣajāgāramiṣyate ||17|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.36.trailer">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.36.trailer</label>
						<caesura/> iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne bhūmipravibhāgīyo nāma
						ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||36|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.1">

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.2">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.37.2</label>
						<caesura/>yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>
					
					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.3">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.37.3</label>
						<caesura/> mātuluṅgyagnimanthau ca bhadradāru mahauṣadham | 
						<caesura/>ahiṃsrā caiva rāsnā ca pralepo vātaśophajit ||3|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.4">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.37.4</label>
						<caesura/> dūrvā ca nalamūlaṃ ca madhukaṃ candanaṃ tathā | 
						<caesura/>śītalāśca gaṇāḥ sarve pralepaḥ pittaśophahṛt ||4|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.5">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.37.5</label>
						<caesura/> āgantuje raktaje ca hyeṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ | 
						<caesura/>vidhir viṣaghno viṣaje pittaghno 'pi hitas tathā ||5|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.6">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.37.6</label>
						<caesura/> ajagandhā'śvagandhā ca kālā saralayā saha | 
						<caesura/>ekaiṣikājaśṛṅgī ca pralepaḥ śleṣmaśophahṛt ||6|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.7">

						<caesura/>anantā ceti lepo 'yaṃ sānnipātikaśophahṛt ||7|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.8">

						<caesura/>pitte, coṣṇaḥ kaphe kṣāramūtrāḍhyastatpraśāntaye ||8|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.9">

						<caesura/>saktavaḥ kiṇvamatasī dravyāṇyuṣṇāni pācanam ||9|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.10">

						<caesura/>kapotakaṅkagṛdhrāṇāṃ purīṣāṇi ca dāraṇam | 
						<caesura/>kṣāradravyāṇi vā yāni kṣāro vā dāraṇaṃ param ||10|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.11">

						<caesura/> kaṅgukā triphalā rodhraṃ kāsīsaṃ śravaṇāhvayā | 
						<caesura/>dhavāśvakarṇayos tvak ca ropaṇaṃ cūrṇamiṣyate ||27|| </l>

						<caesura/> priyaṅgukā sarjarasaḥ puṣpakāsīsam eva ca | 
						<caesura/>tvakcūrṇaṃ dhavajaṃ caiva ropaṇārthaṃ praśasyate ||28|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.29">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.37.29</label>
						<caesura/> tvakṣu nyagrodhavargasya triphalāyās tathaiva ca | 
						<caesura/>rasakriyāṃ ropaṇārthe vidadhīta yathākramam ||29|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.37.30">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.37.30</label>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.3">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.3</label>
						<caesura/> kecid ācāryā bruvate- dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ, kasmāt? vyavasthitatvāt ,
						iha khalu dravyaṃ vyavasthitaṃ na rasādayaḥ, yathā āme phale ye rasādayaste
						pakve na santi; nity atvācca, nityaṃ hi dravyamanity ā guṇāḥ, yathā
						kalkādipravibhāgaḥ, sa eva sampannarasagandho vyāpannarasagandho vā bhavati;
						svajātyavasthānācca, yathā hi pārthivaṃ dravyamanyabhāvaṃ na gacchaty evaṃ
						śeṣāṇi; pañcendriyagrahaṇāśca, pañcabhir indriyairgṛhyate dravyaṃ na
						rasādayaḥ; āśrayatvācca, dravyamāśritā rasādayaḥ; ārambhasāmarthyācca,
						dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ, yathā- ‘vidārigandhādimāhṛtya saṅkṣudya vipacet’ ity
						evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣvārambhaḥ; śāstraprāmāṇyācca, śāstre hi dravyaṃ
						pradhānam upadeśe yogānāṃ, yathā- ‘mātuluṅgāgnimanthau ca’ ity ādau na
						rasādaya upadiśyante; kramāpekṣitatvācca rasādīnāṃ, rasādayo hi
						dravyakramamapekṣante, yathā- taruṇe taruṇāḥ sampūrṇe sampūrṇā iti;
						ekadeśasādhyatvācca, dravyāṇāmekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ sādhyante, yathā-
						mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti; tasmād dravyaṃ pradhānaṃ, na rasādayaḥ, kasmāt?
						niravayavatvāt | dravyalakṣaṇaṃ tu ‘kriyāguṇavat samavāyikāraṇam’ iti ||3|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.4">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.4</label>
						<caesura/> netyāhuranye , rasās tu pradhānaṃ; kasmāt? āgamāt, āgamo hi
						śāstramucyate; śāstre hi rasā adhikṛtāḥ, yathā- rasāyatta āhāra iti, tasmiṃs
						tu prāṇāḥ; upadeśācca, upadiśyante hi rasāḥ, yathā- madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ
						śamayanti; anumānācca, rasena hy anumīyate dravyaṃ, yathā- madhuramiti;
						ṛṣivacanācca, ṛṣivacanaṃ vedo yathā- kiñcidijyārthaṃ madhuramāharediti,
						tasmād rasāḥ pradhānaṃ; raseṣu guṇasañjñā | rasalakṣaṇamanyatropadekṣyāmaḥ
						||4|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.5">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.5</label>
						<caesura/> nety āhur anye , vīryaṃ pradhānam iti | kasmāt?
						tad vaśenauṣadhakarmaniṣpatteḥ |
						ihauṣadhakarmāṇyūrdhvādhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃśodhanasaṃśamanasaṅgrāhikāgnidīpanapīḍanalekhanabṛṃhaṇa-
						rasāyanavājīkaraṇaśvayathukaravilayanadahanadāraṇamādanaprāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanādīni
						vīryaprādhānyādbhavanti | tac ca vīryaṃ dvividhamuṣṇaṃ śītaṃ ca,
						agnīṣomīyatvājjagataḥ | kecid aṣṭavidhamāhuḥ- śītamuṣṇaṃ snigdhaṃ rūkṣaṃ
						viśadaṃ picchilaṃ mṛdu tīkṣṇaṃ ceti | etāni vīryāṇi
						svabalaguṇotkarṣādrasamabhibhūyātmakarma kurvanti | yathā
						tāvanmahatpañcamūlaṃ kaṣāyaṃ tiktānurasaṃ vātaṃ śamayati, uṣṇavīryatvāt ;
						tathā kulatthaḥ kaṣāyaḥ, kaṭukaḥ palāṇḍuḥ, snehabhāvācca; madhuraścekṣuraso
						vātaṃ vardhayati, śītavīryatvāt ; kaṭukā pippalī pittaṃ śamayati,
						mṛduśītavīryatvāt ; amlamāmalakaṃ lavaṇaṃ saindhavaṃ ca; tiktā kākamācī
						pittaṃ vardhayati, uṣṇavīryatvāt , madhurā matsyāśca; kaṭukaṃ mūlakaṃ
						śleṣmāṇaṃ vardhayati, snigdhavīryatvāt ; amlaṃ kapitthaṃ śleṣmāṇāṃ śamayati,
						rūkṣavīryatvāt , madhuraṃ kṣaudraṃ ca; tad etan nidarśanamātram uktam ||5|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.6">

						<caesura/> bhavanti cātra 
						<caesura/> ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
						<caesura/> raukṣyalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam ||6|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.10">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.10</label>
						<caesura/> nety āhur anye , vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt?
						samyaṅmithyāvipakvatvāt ; iha sarvadravāṇyabhyavahṛtāni
						samyaṅmithyāvipakvāni guṇaṃ doṣaṃ vā janayanti | tatrāhuranye- prati rasaṃ
						pāka iti | kecittrividhamicchanti- madhuramamlaṃ kaṭukaṃ ceti | tat tu na
						samyak, bhūtaguṇādāmāccānyo 'mlo vipāko nāsti; pittaṃ hi vidagdhamamlatām
						upaity āgneyatvāt ; yadyevaṃ lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ pāko bhaviṣyati, śleṣmā hi
						vidagdho lavaṇatām upaitīti | madhuro madhurasyāmlo 'mlasyaivaṃ sarveṣām iti
						kecidāhuḥ; dṛṣṭāntaṃ copadiśanti- yathā tāvat kṣīramukhāgataṃ pacyamānaṃ
						madhuram eva syāttathā śāliyavamudgādayaḥ prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvamuttarakāle 'pi
						na parity ajanti tadvaditi | kecidvadanti- abalavanto balavatāṃ
						vaśamāyāntīti | evamanavasthitiḥ, tasmād asiddhānta eṣaḥ | āgame hi dvividha
						eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca | tayor madhurākhyo guruḥ, kaṭukākhyo laghuriti
						| tatra pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyaṃ bhavati guṇasādharmyād gurutā
						laghutā ca; pṛthivyāpaś ca gurvyaḥ, śeṣāṇi laghūni; tasmād dvividha eva pāka
						iti ||10|| </l>

						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.11</label>
						<caesura/> bhavanti cātra
						<caesura/> dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv ambupṛthivīguṇāḥ |
						<caesura/>nirvartante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate ||11||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.14">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.14</label>
						<caesura/> tad dravyam ātmanā kiñcit kiñcid vīryeṇa sevitam |
						<caesura/> kiñcid rasavipākābhyāṃ doṣaṃ hanti karoti vā ||14|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.15">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.15</label>
						<caesura/> pāko nāsti vinā vīryādvīryaṃ nāsti vinā rasāt | 
						<caesura/>raso nāsti vinā dravyāddravyaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtam ||15|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.16">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.16</label>
						<caesura/> janma tu dravyarasayor anyonyāpekṣikaṃ smṛtam | 
						<caesura/>anyonyāpekṣikaṃ janma yathā syād dehadehinoḥ ||16|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.17">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.17</label>
						<caesura/> vīryasañjñā guṇā ye 'ṣṭau te 'pi dravyāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ | 
						<caesura/>raseṣu na bhavanty ete nirguṇās tu guṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ||17||</l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.18">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.18</label>
						<caesura/> dravye dravyāṇi yasmāddhi vipacyante na ṣaḍrasāḥ | 
						<caesura/>śreṣṭhaṃ dravyamato jñeyaṃ, śeṣā bhāvās tad āśrayāḥ ||18|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.19">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.19</label>
						<caesura/> amīmāṃsyāny acintyāni prasiddhāni svabhāvataḥ | 
						<caesura/>āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vicakṣaṇaiḥ ||19|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.20">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.20</label>
						<caesura/> pratyakṣalakṣaṇaphalāḥ prasiddhāś ca svabhāvataḥ |
						<caesura/>nauṣadhīrhetubhir vidvān parīkṣeta kadācana ||20|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.21">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.40.21</label>
						<caesura/> sahasreṇāpi hetūnāṃ nāmbaṣṭhādir virecayet | 
						<caesura/>tasmāt tiṣṭhet tu matimān āgame na tu hetuṣu ||21|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.40.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne
						dravyaguṇarasavīryavipākavijñānīyo nāma catvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||40|| </l>
				</div>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.3">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.3</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ samudāyāddravyābhinirvṛttiḥ, utkarṣastvabhivyañjako
            bhavati- idaṃ pārthivam idam āpyam idaṃ taijasam idaṃ vāyavyam idam ākāśīyam iti ||3|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.1">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.4.1</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra sthūlasāndramandasthiragurukaṭhinaṃ gandhabahulamīṣatkaṣāyaṃ prāyaśo madhuram iti
            pārthivaṃ; tat sthairyabalagauravasaṅghātopacayakaraṃ viśeṣataś cādhogatisvabhāvam iti(1)
            |4| </l>
        	
        	<l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.2">

        		madhurarasaprāyamāpyaṃ; tat snehanahlādanakledanabandhanaviṣyandanakaram iti;(2) |4|</l>
        	
        	<l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.3">

        		viśeṣataścordhvagatisvabhāvam iti taijasaṃ;
        		taddahanapacanadāraṇatāpanaprakāśanaprabhāvarṇakaram iti;(3) |4|</l>
        	
        	<l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.4">

        		vāyavīyaṃ; tadvaiśadyalāghavaglapanavirūkṣaṇavicāraṇakaram iti;(4) |4|</l>
        	
        	<l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.5">

        		tanmārdavaśauṣiryalāghavakaramiti(5) ||4|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.5">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.5</label>
            <caesura/>
             anena nidarśanena nānauṣadhībhūtaṃ jagati kiñcid dravyam astīti kṛtvā taṃ taṃ
            yuktiviśeṣam arthaṃ cābhisamīkṣya svavīryaguṇayuktāni dravyāṇi kārmukāṇi bhavanti | tāni
            yadā kurvanti sa kālaḥ, yat kurvanti tat karma, yena kurvanti tadvīryaṃ, yatra kurvanti
            tad adhikaraṇaṃ, yathā kurvanti sa upāyaḥ, yanniṣpādayanti tat phalamiti ||5|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.6">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.6</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra, virecanadravyāṇi pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni, pṛthivyāpo gurvyaḥ, tāni gurutvād
            adho gacchanti, tasmād virecanamadhoguṇabhūyiṣṭhamanumānāt ;
            vamanadravyāṇyagnivāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni, agnivāyu hi laghū, laghutvācca
            tānyūrdhvamuttiṣṭhanti, tasmād vamanamapyūrdhvaguṇabhūyiṣṭham;
            ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhamubhayatobhāgam; ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ saṃśamanaṃ;
            sāṅgrāhikamanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭham, anilasya śoṣaṇātmakatvāt ; dīpanamagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ,
            tatsamānatvāt ; lekhanamanilānalaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ; bṛṃhaṇaṃ pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭham;
            evamauṣadhakarmāṇyanumānāt sādhayet ||6|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.7">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.7</label>
            <caesura/>
             bhavanti cātra 
          	<caesura/>bhūtejovārijairdravyaiḥ śamaṃ yāti samīraṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhūmyambuvāyujaiḥ pittaṃ kṣipramāpnoti nirvṛtim ||7|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.8">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.8</label>
            <caesura/>
             khatejo 'nilajaiḥ śleṣmā śamameti śarīriṇām | 
          	<caesura/>viyatpavanajātābhyāṃ vṛddhim abhyeti mārutaḥ ||8|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.9">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.9</label>
            <caesura/>
             āgneyam eva yad dravyaṃ tena pittam udīryate | 
          	<caesura/>vasudhājalajātābhyāṃ balāsaḥ parivardhate ||9|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.10">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.10</label>
            <caesura/>
             evam etad guṇādhikyaṃ dravye dravye viniścitam | 
          	<caesura/>dviśo vā bahuśo vā'pi jñātvā doṣeṣu cācaret ||10|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.11">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.11</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra ya ime guṇā vīryasañjñakāḥ śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣamṛdutīkṣṇapicchilaviśadās teṣāṃ
            tīkṣṇoṣṇāvāgneyau, śītapicchilāvambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhau , pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaḥ snehaḥ,
            toyākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ mṛdutvaṃ, vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ raukṣyaṃ,
            kṣitisamīraṇaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vaiśadyaṃ; vipākāvuktaguṇau | tatra, uṣṇasnigdhau vātaghnau,
            śītamṛdupicchilāḥ pittaghnāḥ, tīkṣṇarūkṣaviśadāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ gurupāko vātapittaghnaḥ,
            laghupākaḥ śleṣmaghnaḥ | teṣāṃ mṛduśītoṣṇāḥ sparśagrāhyāḥ, picchilaviśadau
            cakṣuḥsparśābhyāṃ, snigdharūkṣau cakṣuṣā, tīkṣṇo mukhe duḥkhotpādanāt | gurupākaḥ
            sṛṣṭaviṇmūtratayā kaphotkleśena ca, laghurbaddhaviṇmūtratayā mārutakopena ca | tatra
            tulyaguṇeṣu bhūteṣu rasavaiśeṣyam upalakṣayet | tad yathā- madhuro guruśca pārthivaḥ,
            madhuraḥ snigdhaś cāpya iti ||11|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.41.12</label>
            <caesura/>
             bhavati cātra 
          	<caesura/>guṇā ya uktā dravyeṣu śarīreṣv api te tathā |
            <caesura/>
             sthānavṛddhikṣayās tasmād dehināṃ dravyahetukāḥ ||12|| </l>

        	<l xml:id="SS.1.42.1">
        		<label>1938 ed. 1.42.1</label>
        		<caesura/>athāto rasaviśeṣavijñānīyam adhyāyaṃ
        		vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
        	
        	<l xml:id="SS.1.42.2">
        		<label>1938 ed. 1.42.2</label>
        		<caesura/>yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>
          
        	<l xml:id="SS.1.42.3">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.3</label>
            <caesura/>
             ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam ekottaraparivṛddhāḥ
            śabdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ, tasmād āpyo rasaḥ | parasparasaṃsargāt parasparānugrahāt
            parasparānupraveśāc ca sarveṣu sarveṣāṃ sānnidhyamasti, utkarṣāpakarṣāt tu grahaṇam | sa
            khalvāpyo rasaḥ śeṣabhūtasaṃsargādvidagdhaḥ ṣoḍhā vibhajyate; tad yathā- madhuro 'mlo
            lavaṇaḥ kaṭukastiktaḥ kaṣāya iti | te ca bhūyaḥ parasparasaṃsargāttriṣaṣṭidhā bhidyante
            | tatra, bhūmyambuguṇabāhulyānmadhuraḥ, bhūmyagniguṇabāhulyādamlaḥ,
            toyāgniguṇabāhulyāllavaṇaḥ , vāyvagniguṇabāhulyāt kaṭukaḥ, vāyvākāśaguṇabāhulyāttiktaḥ,
            pṛthivyanilaguṇabāhulyāt kaṣāya iti ||3|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.4">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.4</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra, madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaghnāḥ, madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ pittaghnāḥ, kaṭutiktakaṣāyāḥ
            śleṣmaghnāḥ ||4|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.5">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.5</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra vāyor ātmaivātmā, pittamāgneyaṃ, śleṣmā saumya iti ||5|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.6">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.6</label>
            <caesura/>
             ta ete rasāḥ svayonivardhanā, anyayonipraśamanāś ca ||6|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.7">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.7</label>
            <caesura/>
             kecid āhuḥ agnīṣomīyatvāj jagato rasā dvividhāḥ- saumyā āgneyāś ca | madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ
            saumyāḥ; kaṭvamlalavaṇā āgneyāḥ | tatra madhurāmlalavaṇāḥ snigdhā guravaśca,
            kaṭutiktakaṣāyā rūkṣā laghavaśca; saumyāḥ śītāḥ, āgneyā uṣṇāḥ ||7|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.1">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.8.1</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra śaityaraukṣyalāghavavaiśadyavaiṣṭambhyaguṇalakṣaṇo vāyuḥ, tasya samānayoniḥ
            kaṣāyo rasaḥ; so 'sya śaityāc chaityaṃ vardhayati, raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ, lāghavāl lāghavaṃ,
            vaiśadyād vaiśadyaṃ, vaiṣṭambhyād vaiṣṭambhyam iti; (1) |8|</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.2">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.8.2</label>
            <caesura/>
             auṣṇyataikṣṇyaraukṣyalāghavavaiśadyaguṇalakṣaṇaṃ pittaṃ, tasya samānayoniḥ kaṭuko
            rasaḥ; so 'sya auṣṇyād auṣṇyaṃ vardhayati, taikṣṇyāt taikṣṇyaṃ, raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ,
            lāghavāl lāghavaṃ, vaiśadyād vaiśadyam iti (2) |8| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.3">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.8.3</label>
            <caesura/>
             mādhuryasnehagauravaśaityapaicchilyaguṇalakṣaṇaḥ śleṣmā; tasya samānayonir madhuro
            rasaḥ, so 'sya mādhuryānmādhuryaṃ vardhayati, snehāt snehaṃ, gauravād gauravaṃ, śaityāc
            chaity aṃ, paicchilyāt paicchilyam iti (3) ||8|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.4">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.8.4</label>
            <caesura/>
             tasya punaranyayoniḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ; sa śleṣmaṇaḥ pratyanīkatvāt
            kaṭukatvānmādhuryamabhibhavati, raukṣyāt snehaṃ, lāghavād gauravam, auṣṇyāc chaityaṃ,
            vaiśadyāt paicchilyam iti | tad etan nidarśanamātram uktaṃ bhavati (4) ||8|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.9">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.9</label>
            <caesura/>
             rasalakṣaṇam ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ- tatra, yaḥ paritoṣamutpādayati prahlādayati
            tarpayati jīvayati mukhopalepaṃ janayati śleṣmāṇaṃ cābhivardhayati sa madhuraḥ; yo
            dantaharṣam utpādayati mukhāsrāvaṃ janayati śraddhāṃ cotpādayati so 'mlaḥ; yo
            bhaktarucim utpādayati kaphaprasekaṃ janayati mārdavaṃ cāpādayati sa lavaṇaḥ; yo
            jihvāgraṃ bādhate udvegaṃ janayati śiro gṛhṇīte nāsikāṃ srāvayati sa kaṭukaḥ; yo gale
            coṣamutpādayati mukhavaiśadyaṃ janayati bhaktaruciṃ cāpādayati harṣaṃ ca sa tiktaḥ; yo
            vaktraṃ pariśoṣayati jihvāṃ stambhayati kaṇṭhaṃ badhnāti hṛdayaṃ karṣati pīḍayati ca sa
            kaṣāya iti ||9|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.1">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.10.1</label>
            <caesura/>
             rasaguṇān ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ- tatra, madhuro raso rasaraktamāṃsamedo
            'sthimajjaujaḥśukrastanyavardhanaś cakṣuṣyaḥ keśyo varṇyo balakṛtsandhānaḥ
            śoṇitarasaprasādano bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇahitaḥ
            ṣaṭpadapipīlikānāmiṣṭatamastṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhapraśamanaḥ ṣaḍindriyaprasādanaḥ
            kṛmikaphakaraś ceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham āsevyamānaḥ
            kāsaśvāsālasakavamathuvadanamādhuryasvaropaghātakṛmigalagaṇḍānāpādayati
            tathā'rbudaślīpadabastigudopalepābhiṣyandaprabhṛtī ñjanayati(1) |10| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.2">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.10.2</label>
            <caesura/>
             amlo jaraṇaḥ pācano dīpanaḥ pavananigrahaṇo 'nulomanaḥ koṣṭhavidāhī bahiḥśītaḥ kledanaḥ
            prāyaśo hy adyaśceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham upasevyamāno
            dantaharṣanayanasammīlanaromasaṃvejanakaphavilayanaśarīraśaithilyānyāpādayati, tathā
            kṣatābhihatadagdhadaṣṭabhagnarugṇaśūnapracyutāvamūtritavisarpitacchinnabhinnaviddhotpiṣṭādīni
            pācayatyāgneyasvabhāvāt paridahati kaṇṭhamuro hṛdayaṃ ceti(2) |10|</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.3">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.10.3</label>
            <caesura/>
             lavaṇaḥ saṃśodhanaḥ pācano viśleṣaṇaḥ kledanaḥ śaithilyakṛduṣṇaḥ sarvarasapratyanīko
            mārgaviśodhanaḥ sarvaśarīrāvayavamārdavakaraśceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka
            evātyarthamāsevyamāno
            gātrakaṇḍūkoṭhaśophavaivarṇyapuṃstvopaghātendriyopatāpamukhākṣipākaraktapittavātaśoṇitāmlīkāprabhṛtīn āpādayati(3)
            |10| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.4">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.10.4</label>
            <caesura/>
             kaṭuko dīpanaḥ pācano rocanaḥ śodhanaḥ sthaulyālasyakaphakṛmiviṣakuṣṭhakaṇḍūpraśamanaḥ
            sandhibandhavicchedano 'vasādanaḥ stanyaśukramedasām upahantā ceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka
            evātyartham upasevyamāno
            bhramamadagalatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpabalavighātakampatodabhedakṛt
            karacaraṇapārśvapṛṣṭhaprabhṛtiṣu ca vātaśūlān āpādayati(4) |10|</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.5">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.10.5</label>
            <caesura/>
             tiktaśchedano rocano dīpanaḥ śodhanaḥ kaṇḍūkoṭhatṛṣṇāmūrcchājvarapraśamanaḥ
            stanyaśodhano viṇmūtrakledamedovasāpūyopaśoṣaṇaśceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham
            upasevyamāno
            gātramanyāstambhākṣepakārditaśiraḥśūlabhramatodabhedacchedāsyavairasyāny āpādayati(5)
            |10| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.6">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.10.6</label>
            <caesura/>
             kaṣāyaḥ saṅgrāhako ropaṇaḥ stambhanaḥ śodhano lekhanaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ pīḍanaḥ
            kledopaśoṣaṇaś ceti; sa evaṅguṇo 'pyeka evātyartham upasevyamāno
            hṛtpīḍāsyaśoṣodarādhmānavākyagrahamanyāstambha-
            gātrasphuraṇacumucumāyanākuñcanākṣepaṇaprabhṛtī ñjanayati ||10|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.11">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.11</label>
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarveṣām eva dravyāṇyupadekṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā- kākolyādiḥ
            kṣīraghṛtavasāmajjaśāliṣaṣṭikayavagodhūmamāṣaśṛṅgāṭakakaserukatrapusair
            vārukarkārukālābūkālindakataka-
            giloḍyapriyālapuṣkarabījakāśmaryamadhūkadrākṣākharjūrarājādanatālanālikerekṣuvikārabalātibalātmaguptā-
            vidārīpayasyāgokṣurakakṣīramoraṭamadhūlikākūṣmāṇḍaprabhṛtīni samāsena madhuro vargaḥ;
            dāḍimāmalakamātuluṅgāmrātakakapitthakaramardabadarakolaprācīnāmalakatintiḍīkakośāmrakabhavyapārāvata-
            vetraphalalakucāmlavetasadantaśaṭhadadhitakrasurāśuktasauvīrakatuṣodakadhānyāmlaprabhṛtīni
            samāsenāmlo vargaḥ;
            saindhavasauvarcalaviḍapākyaromakasāmudrakapaktrimayavakṣāroṣaraprasūtasuvarcikāprabhṛtīni
            samāsena lavaṇo vargaḥ; pippalyādiḥ surasādiḥ
            śigrumadhuśigrumūlakalaśunasumukhaśītaśivakuṣṭhadevadāruhareṇukāvālgujaphala-
            caṇḍāguggulumustalāṅgalakīśukanāsāpīluprabhṛtīni sālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ kaṭuko vargaḥ;
            āragvadhādirguḍūcyādirmaṇḍūkaparṇīvetrakarīraharidrādvayendrayavavaruṇasvādukaṇṭakasaptaparṇabṛhatīdvayaśaṅkhinīdravantī-
            trivṛtkṛtavedhanakarkoṭakakāravellavārtākakarīrakaravīrasumanaḥśaṅkhapuṣpyapāmārgatrāyamāṇāśokarohiṇīvaijayantī-
            suvarcalāpunarnavāvṛścikālījyotiṣmatīprabhṛtīni samāsena tikto vargaḥ;
            nyagrodhādirambaṣṭhādiḥ priyaṅgvādī
            rodhrādistriphalāśallakījambvāmrabakulatindukaphalāni
            katakaśākaphalapāṣāṇabhedakavanaspatiphalāni sālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ
            kuruvakakovidārakajīvantīcillīpālaṅkyāsuniṣaṇṇakaprabhṛtīni varakādayo mudgādayaś ca
            samāsena kaṣāyo vargaḥ ||11|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.12">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.12</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatraiteṣāṃ rasānāṃ saṃyogāstriṣaṣṭirbhavanti | tad yathā- pañcadaśa dvikāḥ,
            viṃśatistrikāḥ, pañcadaśa catuṣkāḥ, ṣaṭ pañcakāḥ, ekaśaḥ ṣaḍrasāḥ, ekaḥ ṣaṭka iti |
            teṣāṃ anyatra prayojanāni vakṣyāmaḥ ||12|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.13">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.42.13</label>
            <caesura/>
             bhavati cātra 
          	<caesura/>jagdhāḥ ṣaḍadhigacchanti balino vaśyatāṃ rasāḥ | 
          	<caesura/>yathā prakupitā doṣā vaśaṃ yānti balīyasaḥ ||13|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.42.trailer">iti suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne rasaviśeṣavijñānīyo nāma dvicatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ

             vamanadravyāṇāṃ phalādīnāṃ madanaphalāni śreṣṭhatamāni bhavanti | atha
            madanapuṣpāṇāmātapapariśuṣkāṇāṃ cūrṇaprakuñjaṃ
            pratyakpuṣpāsadāpuṣpīnimbakaṣāyāṇāmanyatamenāloḍya madhusaindhavayuktāṃ puṣpacūrṇamātrāṃ
            pāyayitvā vāmayet | madanaśalāṭucūrṇānyevaṃ vā bakularamyakopayuktāni
            madhulavaṇayuktānyabhiprataptāni; madanaśalāṭucūrṇasiddhāṃ vā tilataṇḍulayavāgūm |
            nirvṛttānāṃ vā nātiharitapāṇḍūnāṃ kuśamūḍhāvabaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
            yavabu(tu)ṣamudgamāṣaśālyādidhānyarāśāvaṣṭarātroṣitaklinnabhinnānāṃ phalānāṃ
            phalapippalīruddhṛtyātape śoṣayet, tāsāṃ dadhimadhupalalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ
            subhājanasthānāmantarnakhamuṣṭimuṣṇe yaṣṭīmadhukakaṣāye kovidārādīnāmanyatame vā kaṣāye
            pramṛdya rātriparyuṣitaṃ madhusaindhavayuktamāśīrbhir abhimantritamudaṅmukhaḥ

          	<caesura/>maṇḍodakārthe kvāthaṃ ca dadyāt tat sarvam ekataḥ ||33||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.34">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.44.34</label>
            <caesura/>
             nidadhyāt kalase tāṃ tu surāṃ jātarasāṃ pibet | 
          	<caesura/>eṣa eva surākalpo vamaneṣv api kīrtitaḥ ||34||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.35">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.44.35</label>
            <caesura/>
             mūlāni trivṛdādīnāṃ prathamasya gaṇasya ca | 
          	<caesura/>mahataḥ pañcamūlasya mūrvāśārṅgaṣṭayor api ||35|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.36">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.44.36</label>
            <caesura/>
             sudhāṃ haimavatīṃ caiva triphalātiviṣe vacām | 
          	<caesura/>saṃhṛtyaitāni bhāgau dvau kārayed ekam etayoḥ ||36|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.37">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.44.37</label>
            <caesura/>
             kuryān niḥkvātham ekasminn ekasmiṃś cūrṇam eva tu | 
          	<caesura/>kṣuṇṇāṃs tasmiṃs tu niḥkvāthe bhāvayed bahuśo yavān ||37|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.38">

            <caesura/>

          	<caesura/>caturthaṃ bhāgamāvāpya cūrṇānāmatra kīrtitam ||38|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.39">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.44.39</label>
            <caesura/>
             prakṣipya kalase samyak tatastaṃ tadanantaram | 
          	<caesura/>teṣāṃ eva kaṣāyeṇa śītalena suyojitam ||39|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.40">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.44.40</label>
            <caesura/>
             pūrvavat sannidadhyāt tu jñeyaṃ sauvīrakaṃ hi tat |
          	<caesura/>pūrvoktaṃ vargam āhṛtya dvidhā kṛtvaikam etayoḥ ||40|| </l>

        	<l xml:id="SS.1.44.41">

        		<caesura/>ajaśṛṅgyāḥ kaṣāyeṇa tamabhyāsicya sādhayet ||41|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.42">

          	<caesura/>vimṛdya satuṣān samyak tatastān pūrvavan mitān ||42||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.44">

          <l xml:id="SS.1.44.46">

        <div n="45" type="adhyāya">

        	<l xml:id="SS.1.45.1">
        		<label>1938 ed. 1.45.1</label>
        		<caesura/> athāto dravadravyavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
        			|| </l>
        		
        	<l xml:id="SS.1.45.2">
        		<label>1938 ed. 1.45.2</label>
        		<caesura/> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.3">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.45.3</label>
            <caesura/>
             pānīyamāntarīkṣamanirdeśyarasamamṛtaṃ jīvanaṃ tarpaṇaṃ dhāraṇamāśvāsajananaṃ
            śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrānidrādāhapraśamanamekāntataḥ pathyatamaṃ ca ||3|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.45.4</label>
            <caesura/>
             tad evāvanipatitam anyatamaṃ rasam upalabhate
            sthānaviśeṣān nadīnadasarastaḍāgavāpīkūpacuṇṭīprasravaṇodbhidavikirakedārapalvalādiṣu
            sthāneṣv avasthitam iti ||4|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.45.5</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatra lohitakapilapāṇḍunīlapītaśukleṣv avanipradeśeṣu
            madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyāṇi yathāsaṅkhyam udakāni sambhavanti’ ity eke bhāṣante
            ||5|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.45.6</label>
            <caesura/>
             tat tu na samyak pṛthivyādīnāmanyonyānupraveśakṛtaḥ salilaraso bhavatyutkarṣāpakarṣeṇa
            | tatra, svalakṣaṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmāvamlaṃ lavaṇaṃ ca ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ madhuraṃ;
            tejoguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ kaṭukaṃ tiktaṃ ca vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ kaṣāyam;
            ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāmavyaktarasam, avyaktaṃ hyākāśamity ataḥ; tat
            pradhānamavyaktarasatvāt tat peyam āntarīkṣālābhe ||6|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7">
            <label>1938 ed. 1.45.7</label>
            <caesura/>
             tatrāntarīkṣaṃ caturvidham | tad yathā dhāraṃ, kāraṃ, tauṣāraṃ, haimam iti | teṣāṃ
            dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ, laghutvāt ; tat punardvividhaṃ- gāṅgaṃ, sāmudraṃ ceti | tatra
            gāṅgamāśvayuje māsi prāyaśo varṣati | tayor dvayor api parīkṣaṇaṃ kurvīta-
            śālyodanapiṇḍamakuthitamavidagdhaṃ rajatabhājanopahitaṃ varṣati deve bahiṣkurvīta, sa
            yadi muhūrtaṃ sthitastādṛśa eva bhavati tadā gāṅgaṃ patatītyavagantavyaṃ; varṇānyatve
            sikthapraklede ca sāmudram iti vidyāt, tannopādeyam | sāmudramapyāśvayuje māsi gṛhītaṃ
            gāṅgavadbhavati | gāṅgaṃ punaḥ pradhānaṃ, tadupādadītāśvayuje māsi |
            śuciśuklavitatapaṭaikadeśacyutamathavā harmyatalaparibhraṣṭamanyair vā śucibhir
            bhājanairgṛhītaṃ sauvarṇe rājate mṛnmaye vā pātre nidadhyāt | tat sarvakālam upayuñjīta,
            tasyālābhe bhaumam | taccākāśaguṇabahulam | tat punaḥ saptavidham | tad yathā- kaupaṃ,
            nādeyaṃ, sārasaṃ, tāḍāgaṃ, prāsravaṇam, audbhidaṃ, cauṇṭyam iti ||7|| </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8">

             tatra varṣāsvāntarikṣamaudbhidaṃ vā seveta, mahāguṇatvāt ; śaradi sarvaṃ, prasannatvāt
            hemante sārasaṃ tāḍāgaṃ vā; vasante kaupaṃ prāsravaṇaṃ vā; grīṣme 'pyevaṃ; prāvṛṣi
            cauṇṭyamanabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ ceti ||8|| </l>

            raviśaśikiraṇānilairnābhijuṣṭaṃ gandhavarṇarasopasṛṣṭaṃ tadvyāpannam iti vidyāt | tasya
            sparśarūparasagandhavīryavipākadoṣāḥ ṣaṭ sambhavanti | tatra, kharatā paicchilyam auṣṇyaṃ
            dantagrāhitā ca sparśadoṣaḥ, paṅkasikatāśaivālabahuvarṇatā rūpadoṣaḥ; vyaktarasatā
            rasadoṣaḥ; aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ; yad upayuktaṃ

            chinnabhinnaviddhotpiṣṭacyutamathitakṣatapiccitabhagnasphuṭitakṣārāgnidagdhaviśliṣṭadāritā
            bhihatadurbhagnamṛgavyālavidaṣṭaprabhṛtiṣu ca pariṣekābhyaṅgāvagāhādiṣu tilatailaṃ

          <caesura/>madhu tu madhuraṃ kaṣāyānurasaṃ rūkṣaṃ śītamagnidīpanaṃ varṇyaṃ
            svaryaṃ laghu sukumāraṃ lekhanaṃ hṛdyaṃ vājīkaraṇaṃ sandhānaṃ śodhanaṃ ropaṇaṃ(saṅgrāhi
            ) cakṣuṣyaṃ prasādanaṃ sūkṣmamārgānusāri
            pittaśleṣmamedomehahikkāśvāsakāsātisāraccharditṛṣṇākṛmiviṣapraśamanaṃ hlādi
            tridoṣapraśamanaṃ ca; tat tu laghutvāt kaphaghnaṃ, paicchilyān mādhuryāt kaṣāyabhāvāc ca
            vātapittaghnam ||132|| </l>

	<div n="46" type="adhyāya">

          <l xml:id="SS.1.46.1">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.1</label> athāto 'nnapānavidhim adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ
						|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.2">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.2</label> yathovāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.3">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.3</label>
						<caesura/> dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca- prāgabhihitaḥ ‘prāṇināṃ
						punarmūlamāhāro balavarṇaujasāṃ ca, sa ṣaṭsu raseṣvāyattaḥ, rasāḥ
						punardravyāśrayiṇaḥ,’ dravyarasaguṇavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī
						doṣāṇāṃ sāmyaṃ ca, brahmāderapi ca lokasyāhāraḥ sthity utpattivināśahetuḥ,
						āhārādevābhivṛddhirbalamārogyaṃ varṇendriyaprasādaśca, tathā
						hyāhāravaiṣamyādasvāsthyaṃ; tasyāśitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
						nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpasyānekavidhaprabhāvasya pṛthak
						pṛthagdravyarasaguṇavīryavipākakarmāṇīcchāmi jñātuṃ, na hy
						anavabuddhasvabhāvā bhiṣajaḥ svasthānuvṛttiṃ roganigrahaṇaṃ ca kartuṃ
						samarthāḥ; āhārāyattāś ca sarvaprāṇino yasmāttasmād annapānavidhim upadiśatu
						me bhagavānity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ- atha khalu vatsa
						suśruta! yathāpraśnamucyamānam upadhārayasva- ||3|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.4">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.4</label>
						<caesura/> tatra,
						lohitaśālikalamakardamakapāṇḍukasugandhakaśakunāhṛtapuṣpāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukarodhrapuṣpaka-
						dīrghaśūkakāñcanakamahiṣamahāśūkahāyanakadūṣakamahādūṣakaprabhṛtayaḥ śālayaḥ
						||4|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.5">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.5</label>
						<caesura/> madhurā vīryataḥ śītā laghupākā balāvahāḥ |
						<caesura/>pittaghnālpānilakaphāḥ snigdhā baddhālpavarcasaḥ ||5|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.6">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.6</label>
						<caesura/> teṣāṃ lohitakaḥ śreṣṭho doṣaghnaḥ śukramūtralaḥ |
						<caesura/>cakṣuṣyo varṇabalakṛt svaryo hṛdyastṛṣāpahaḥ ||6|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.7">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.7</label>
						<caesura/> vraṇyo jvaraharaś caiva sarvadoṣaviṣāpahaḥ <caesura/> tasmād
						alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśaḥ śālayo 'varāḥ ||7|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.8">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.8</label>
						<caesura/>
						ṣaṣṭikakāṅgukamukundakapītakapramodakakākalakāsanapuṣpakamahāṣaṣṭikacūrṇakakuravakakedāraprabhṛtayaḥ
						ṣaṣṭikāḥ ||8|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.9">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.9</label>
						<caesura/> rase pāke ca madhurāḥ śamanā vātapittayoḥ | <caesura/>śālīnāṃ ca
						guṇais tulyā bṛṃhaṇāḥ kaphaśukralāḥ ||9|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.10">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.10</label>
						<caesura/> ṣaṣṭikaḥ pravaras teṣāṃ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ | <caesura/>mṛduḥ
						snigdhastridoṣaghnaḥ sthairyakṛdbalavardhanaḥ ||10|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.11">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.11</label>
						<caesura/> vipāke madhuro grāhī tulyo lohitaśālibhiḥ <caesura/>
						śeṣāstvalpāntarāstasmāt ṣaṣṭikāḥ kramaśo guṇaiḥ ||11|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.12">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.12</label>
						<caesura/>
						kṛṣṇavrīhiśālāmukhajatumukhanandīmukhalāvākṣakatvaritakakukkuṭāṇḍakapārāvatakapāṭalaprabhṛtayo
						vrīhayaḥ ||12|| </l>

						<caesura/> tatra pūrvaśasyajātānāṃ badarāmlaṃ, vaidalānāṃ dhānyāmlaṃ,
						jaṅghālānāṃ dhanvajānāṃ ca pippalyāsavaḥ, viṣkirāṇāṃ kolabadarāsavaḥ,
						pratudānāṃ kṣīravṛkṣāsavaḥ, guhāśayānāṃ kharjūranālikerāsavaḥ,
						prasahānāmaśvagandhāsavaḥ, parṇamṛgāṇāṃ kṛṣṇagandhāsavaḥ, bileśayānāṃ
						phalāsavaḥ , ekaśaphānāṃ triphalāsavaḥ, anekaśaphānāṃ khadirāsavaḥ,
						kūlacarāṇāṃ śṛṅgāṭakakaśerukāsavaḥ, kośavāsināṃ pādināṃ ca sa eva,
						plavānāmikṣurasāsavaḥ, nādeyānāṃ matsyānāṃ mṛṇālāsavaḥ, sāmudrāṇāṃ
						mātuluṅgāsavaḥ, amlānāṃ phalānāṃ padmotpalakandāsavaḥ, kaṣāyāṇāṃ
						dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ, madhurāṇāṃ trikaṭukayuktaḥ khaṇḍāsavaḥ, tālaphalādīnāṃ
						dhānyāmlaṃ, kaṭukānāṃ dūrvānalavetrāsavaḥ, pippalyādīnāṃ
						śvadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ, kūṣmāṇḍādīnāṃ dārvīkarīrāsavaḥ, cuccuprabhṛtīnāṃ
						lodhrāsavaḥ, jīvantyādīnāṃ triphalāsavaḥ, kusumbhaśākasya sa eva,
						maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnāṃ mahāpañcamūlāsavaḥ, tālamastakādīnāmamlaphalāsavaḥ,
						saindhavādīnāṃ surāsava āranālaṃ ca, toyaṃ vā sarvatreti ||433|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.532">

						<caesura/> imaṃ vidhiṃ yo 'numataṃ mahāmunernṛparṣimukhyasya paṭheddhi yatnataḥ | 
						<caesura/>sa bhūmipālāya vidhātumauṣadhaṃ mahātmanāṃ cārhati sūrisattamaḥ ||532|| </l>

					<l xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer">
						<label>1938 ed. 1.46.trailer</label>
						<caesura/> iti bhagavatā śrīdhanvantariṇopadiṣṭāyāṃ tacchiṣyeṇa maharṣiṇā
						suśrutena viracitāyāṃ suśrutasaṃhitāyāṃ sūtrasthāne ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamo
						'dhyāyaḥ ||46|| </l>
